[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run of `exif_from_data_fuzzer` uncovered a heap-buffer-overflow in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif library. AddressSanitizer reports a one-byte out-of-bounds read in the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `exif_get_sshort` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min exif-utils.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, triggered during the loading of Apple[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note data [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_load`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while parsing EXIF metadata.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Memory safety vulnerability: heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The fuzzer executed `exif_from_data_fuzzer` against a testcase.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - During the EXIF parsing workflow, libexif allocated a [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte buffer for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - A subsequent call to `exif_get_sshort` attempted to read one byte past the end [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof that buffer, triggering AddressSanitizer’s heap-buffer-overflow check and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maborting execution.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x515000000785[0m[39m`, which is [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes beyond the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m512[0m[39m-byte allocation.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The immediate stack frame is:  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
